msg:Went in early August. I did a little homework before going, so I chose to live in Gaozhuang Scenic Area. This is a correct choice because it is indeed more convenient to live in the scenic area. But my homework was not enough, so I made some mistakes. First of all, when Ctrip searched for the five-star scenic spot, it only jumped out of this hotel, but it is not a five-star, but a private hotel with slightly better hardware, which is incomparable to a real five-star hotel. However, there are no real five-star hotels in the scenic area. They are all private hotels. Then there is the choice of location. According to locals, we live in the newly developed fifth district of the scenic spot. In the first half of this year, there was a sudden fire in Xishuangbanna, so many hotels and homestays began to be launched. This district is full of projects under construction. When we stayed in this hotel, as soon as we entered the room, there was a hotel under construction just across the alley. The sound of the electric drill could be heard clearly, and the hotel staff said it was okay, and the renovation was not done at night. However, there was a pungent chemical smell permeating the room at another construction site that was not being painted or glued by a wall next to it. We felt that it was totally unacceptable to live in. We asked if we could change to the opposite room. The hotel responded that the opposite room is a river-view room. If you want to add money, you will check out for free if you don‚Äôt want to. We think this is a bit unreasonable. This is entirely due to the influence of the surrounding environment of the hotel, which makes the room unsuitable for living. We don't want to enjoy a river view room, but just want a normal room without pollution. Finally, under the communication of Ctrip, one hotel was upgraded for free, and the other one still required us to add money. Ctrip subsidized half of the additional money. Thinking of coming, just live. But after staying for a while, I felt that although the smell in the room was small, but the smell in the aisle was very big. As a result, the hotel said that he had checked in and could not check out for free, so he had to go out and look for houses on the street again under the scorching sun, and found another one, and agreed to move in the next day. I saw several here, and stayed here for one night and another for three nights. I feel that this hardware is relatively good in this area, whether it is swimming pool, breakfast, free drinks and fruits. But after all, it is a private hotel, and the service, management and hardware still cannot match the real chain hotel. The decoration around the hotel has a great impact, and we did not inform in advance, which made us waste a lot of time and energy to find the hotel temporarily. This year, due to the impact of the epidemic, business in all hotels is very bleak. The floor where we live seems to be only our family, so I think they may not want to lose their hard-earned customers and did not inform in advance of the impact of the decoration. But in that case, it is more important to retain customers through value-added services, rather than making customers pay for the negative impact of construction around the hotel
